A background server does all the work by receiving the spoken phrase from Cortana, and then providing Cortana a sentence to read back.\r\n\r\nSince the app uses an HTTP connection, it means sensitive home automation commands will not be encrypted (see warranty section under Additional Terms for more information).\r\n\r\nThis app will send a text string representing what was spoken to your Premise server.  Your Premise Home Control server does all the processing via my SpeechParser module (download for free from my YouTube channel).  The SpeechParser command phrases are easily customized, and are NOT order dependent.  End user setup for the SpeechParser module is straight forward, and covered in tutorial video numbers 7.x on my YouTube channel.\r\n\r\nIf you want to use this app on the same machine as your Premise server, you need to enable a network loopback for this app on your Windows machine; in this manner the app will have access to localhost.
